function logoHighlighter(){
		var logos_slider = document.querySelectorAll('[aria-hidden="false"]');
		if(logos_slider != undefined){
			logos_slider.forEach((logo_slider) => {
			logo_slider.classList.add('logo_border_shadow');
			});
			var middle = logos_slider.length % 2;
			middle = (logos_slider.length % 2 == 0) ? middle+2 : middle+1;
	    	if(logos_slider.length <= 3) {
				middle = 1
			}
			if(logos_slider[middle] != undefined){
			logos_slider[middle].classList.remove('logo_border_shadow');	
			}
			
		}
	}


setInterval(logoHighlighter, 500);
	
logoHighlighter();
